england kaa aakhri wicket 45wein over kii duusari gend par fin ke rup main gira
 For Australia, mckay took three wickets, Johnson took two and Foakner, Adam Voges, Ahmed and Watson took one wicket each
 isse pehle toss harkar ballebaaji karne utari australian pari kii shuruyaat wicket ke saath hui, lekin madhyakram kii sadhi hui gendbaaji kii badaulat usne nirdhaarit 50 overon main saat wicket ke nuksaan par 315 ranon kaa vishaal score khadaa kar liya
 Australian opener Shaun Marsh was caught behind the wicket at zero total without opening the account
 iske baad aaron finch (45) or watasan (38) ne duusare wicket kii saajhedaari main 60 ran jodakar team ko sthirataa pradaan kii
 finch-watson pair was broken by Ravi Bopara
 watsan, bopaara kii gend par wicket ke peeche butler ke haathon lapke gaye
 After Watson left, Finch also shared a 56-run partnership with captain Clarke
 finch ko james tradewell ne 22wein over kii paanchavi gend par joe root ke haathon lapakvaaya
 Finch missed the half-century by five runs
 unhone itani hi gendon main chaar chauke or ek chakka jadaa
 After Finch departed, Australia had the most successful partnership for the fourth wicket
 clark ne jorge baile (82) ke saath 130 gendon main tej 155 ran banaakar australia ko majboot score kii ore agrasar kiya
 Although Ballet could not score a century and caught Treadwell off Bopara, but he scored fast runs for the team
 baile ne 67 gendon kaa saamana kiya or paanch chauke tathaa chaar chakka lagaaya
 Shortly after the departure of the ballet, Clarke also caught a catch behind the wicket of Boyd Rankin
 tippaniyan For England, Bopara, Rankin and Stuart Finn took two wickets each, and Treadwell took one wicket each
 paanch maichon kii is shrunkhlaa kaa pehla match barish kii bhent chadh gaya, or is jeet ke saath hi australia ne siries par 1-0 se badhat bana lee he
 Australia lost the toss and batted first, thanks to a brilliant century by captain Michael Clarke (105), a huge target of 316 in front of England, then bowled excellently to 44 the entire England team
 2 overon main 227 ranon par dhwast kar diya
 Clarke, the hero of Australia's victory, hit 14 fours in 102 balls
 australia se mili vishaal lakshya kaa dabaav england par shuru se dikhaai diya or england ke salaami ballebaajon ne atirikt sajagata baratate hue behad dhimi shuruyaat kii
 The England opener could not even open the account in the first two overs, and lost the first wicket in the fifth ball of the fourth over as Michael Carberry (4)
 agali hi gend par jonathan trot bhi shunya ko nijee score par wicket ke peeche lapke gaye
 By the 11th over, England's third wicket had also fallen
 iske baad behad mushkil paristhitiyon main kevin petersan (60) or captain ian morgan (54) ne apni ardhshtkeey pariyon kii badaulat team ko sanbhaalane kii puri koshish kii, lekin is bich aavashyak ran rate badhata chalaa gaya
 Pietersen was caught by Shane Watson at the hands of James Faulkner on the first ball of the 22nd over
 petersan ne 66 gendon kaa saamana kar chah chauke or do chakka lagaaya
 At the same time, Morgan faced four fours in 69 balls before he was caught by Clint mckay
 england ke liye agali sangharshabhari pari wicketiper josh butler (75) ne kheli
 Butler added 47 runs in a ninth wicket partnership with Stuart Finn (16)
 47 ranon kii is saajhedaari main butler ne akele 41 ranon kaa yogadan diya
 Butler was caught by Fawah Ahmed in the second ball of the 44th over by Mitchell Johnson
 butler ne 65 gendon main paanch chauke or teen chakke lagaae
 England's last wicket fell as Finn on the second ball of the 45th over
 australia ke liye maike ne teen, johnson ne do tathaa foxnar, adam vogs, ahamed or watasan ne ek-ek wicket hasil kiya
 Earlier, losing the toss and batting, the Australian innings started with a wicket, but thanks to the middle-order bowling, he scored a huge 315 runs at the loss of seven wickets in the prescribed 50 overs
 australia ke salaami ballebaaj shaun marsh bina khaataa khole shunya ke kul yoga par wicket ke peeche lapke gaye
 Aaron Finch (45) and Watson (38) then added 60 runs in the second wicket partnership to provide stability to the team
 finch-watsan kii jodi ko ravi bopaara ne todaa
 Watson was caught by Butler behind the wicket off Bopara
 watsan ke jane ke baad finch ne captain clark ke saath bhi 56 ranon kii saajhedaari nibhaai
 Finch was caught by James Treadwell on the fifth ball of the 22nd over by Joe Root
 finch paanch ran se ardhshtak se chook gaye
 He hit four fours and a six in the same balls
 finch ke jane ke baad chauthe wicket ke liye australia kii sabase safal saajhedaari hui
 Clarke scored a quick 155 off 130 balls with George Ballet (82) leading Australia to a strong score
 baile haalanki shatak nahin bana sake or bopaara kii gend par tradewell ko kaich thama baithe, lekin team ke liye unhone teji se ran jutaaye
 Ballet faced 67 balls and hit five fours and four sixes
 baile ke jane ke kuch hi der baad clark bhi boid rankin kii gend par wicket ke peeche kaich thama baithe
 The comments england ke liye bopaara, rankin or stuart fin ne do-do wicket, tathaa tradewell ne ek wicket hasil kiya
 The first match of this five-match series was rained out, and with this victory Australia has taken a 1-0 lead over the series
